Product Description

   This popular classic strain was originally developed in the United
   States to cross the pure indica genetics of an Afghani strain with the
   durable genes of Skunk plants. Afghan Skunk quickly spread to Amsterdam
   and beyond and is now considered one of the “classics.”

Product Description

   This popular classic strain was originally developed in the United
   States to cross the pure indica genetics of an Afghani strain with the
   durable genes of Skunk plants. Afghan Skunk quickly spread to Amsterdam
   and beyond and is now considered one of the “classics.”

Product Description

   This popular classic strain was originally developed in the United
   States to cross the pure indica genetics of an Afghani strain with the
   durable genes of Skunk plants. Afghan Skunk quickly spread to Amsterdam
   and beyond and is now considered one of the “classics.”
